To Be Sent to Hong Kong Today

The Changxing Company's ship "Empress of Canada" from Vancouver to Shanghai, when the ship arrived in Japan, a Philippine passenger named Bi Laisi went crazy inside the large rudder and entered the steerage cabin with a knife, slashing anyone he encountered. Who is the Floating Corpse? 188

Wang Ahua Goes Missing, Father Identifies the Body

Land Protector Collects the Body Without Reporting, Too Confused

Wang Ahua, a resident of Yuepu, Wusong, was helping out at Gao Yisheng's house and then went missing. Later, a male corpse floated up in Pudong and was collected by the land protector. Recently, Wang's father, Wang Fengzhou, came forward to accuse Gao Yisheng and others of beating his son to death and throwing him into the river to cover up their tracks. He claimed that the corpse was his son. The first precinct of the seventh district arrested Gao Yisheng and handed him over to the local court for detention. However, the defendant claimed that the corpse collected by the land protector was an unidentified floating corpse and that Wang Fengzhou was falsely claiming kinship. The court stated that since the land protector had retrieved the male corpse at the time, why did he not report it for identification? It was obvious that he was confused in his handling of the matter and that there were suspicious points. Therefore, he had ordered an investigation. However, the corpse had already decomposed and it would not be easy to identify it without exhuming the body. Who it is is truly a mystery.

Shanghai South Public Bus Disturbance Yesterday 189

Soldiers Causing Trouble on the Bus

The Daily News reports that yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, a Route 3 circular bus of the Shanghai South Public Bus Company, traveling from Xiaodongmen to the Xinqiao Street station, was boarded by a soldier from the machine gun company of the 26th Regiment stationed in Longhua. The female ticket seller, Lu Dongmei, asked him to purchase a ticket. The soldier claimed he was on official duty and had never bought a ticket on any bus. The ticket seller stated that there were regulations for military personnel riding buses, and if on official assignment, she requested to see his official document to comply with the regulations. The soldier replied that he was carrying important documents and could not disclose confidential information to the public. The two sides argued, and the female ticket seller was slapped by the soldier. When the bus arrived at Laoximen, the soldier jumped off, intending to escape, but the ticket seller grabbed him and took him to the bus company. The company telegraphed the 26th Regiment, which instructed them to bring the soldier to the regiment for questioning. The company's investigator and the female ticket seller then escorted the soldier to the regiment. However, when they reached Huasheng Bridge, they were surrounded by many soldiers from the regiment. The patrol police in the area, upon hearing of this, reported to the Second District Public Security Bureau. Inspector Gao led several police officers to mediate. However, the soldiers were overbearing, refusing to listen to reason and even attempting to assault the police officers. Inspector Gao, outnumbered, was helpless. The Public Security Bureau telegraphed the 26th Regiment, requesting officers to come to the scene to suppress the situation. Deputy Officer Deng of the regiment then led several soldiers to the scene and took the soldier who had caused the disturbance on the bus away for investigation. The others dispersed in a rush. Deputy Officer Deng, fearing other soldiers would seek revenge, deployed armed soldiers on each bus for protection.

Riverside Shacks Already Dismantled Yesterday

The Daily News reports that the Shanghai Municipal Civilian Housing Committee is making every effort to provide housing for the city's poor. There are over four hundred shacks along the riverside in that area, but due to habit, they have not yet moved. Yesterday, the committee dismantled about two hundred of the riverside shacks, ordering the residents to move. Chang Yunheng Sues Ling Bao and Zhi Zun Bao 193

Seeking Damages of Seven Thousand Two Hundred Yuan

Chang Yunheng, backstage manager of the Tianchan Stage, filed a lawsuit with the Special District Court accusing Gu Er Kang, manager of Ling Bao and Zhi Zun Bao located at 308 Ningbo Road, of defamation. The complaint stated that the plaintiff, as backstage manager of Tianchan Stage, never improperly took a single coin from the performers beyond his regular salary. However, Ling Bao and Zhi Zun Bao, for unknown reasons, fabricated false claims, publishing groundless stories that intentionally damaged the plaintiff's reputation. The articles alleged that the plaintiff received kickbacks from each performer's monthly salary. Specifically, it claimed that although Qilin Tong's salary was three thousand one hundred yuan, the plaintiff received the full amount each month and, dissatisfied with not receiving the odd hundred yuan as a reward, sought to vent his anger by creating difficulties and withholding the salary for the month, leading Zhou (Qilin Tong) to consider leaving Tianchan (as seen in Ling Bao issue 122 and Zhi Zun Bao issue 1). Gu Zhuxuan, owner of Tianchan Stage, believing the report to be true, became enraged, immediately suspended the plaintiff from his position as backstage manager, and ordered him to clear his accounts, return all kickbacks received from the performers over time, or he would not be allowed to go elsewhere. The plaintiff argued that the newspapers fabricated facts and spread rumors, damaging his reputation and causing him to be unjustly suspended, constituting a violation of Article 330 of the Criminal Code. As the backstage manager of Tianchan Stage, he received a monthly salary of six hundred yuan. Due to the impact of the false reports, he has lost his job and cannot expect to be hired elsewhere. Being unemployed for a year results in a loss of seven thousand two hundred yuan, and ten years would amount to seventy-two thousand yuan. He is therefore claiming damages of seven thousand two hundred yuan based on one year's loss. The trial was scheduled for yesterday, but the defendant could not be served as the summons was delivered by a Chinese constable who reported that the address on Ningbo Road did not exist. The plaintiff also failed to appear due to other matters. The case was adjourned to a later date.

Inmates Universally Vaccinated 194

Dong Changmin, warden of the Jiangsu Second Prison in Caohejing, recently stated that with the arrival of summer and the overcrowding of inmates in the prison, hygiene should be given more attention. To prevent the outbreak of epidemics, he requested the Municipal Health Bureau to send physicians Yang Yujie, Li Minsheng, and Zhang Wenkui to the prison on the 8th of this month to administer vaccinations. Over two thousand male and female inmates in the entire prison were universally vaccinated, a task that took a full day to complete.

Ju Runsheng Sued for Ignoring Advances Case 195

Witness Testimony Already Heard

Re-scheduled for Further Arguments

Zhao Guanqing, previously having retained lawyers Zheng Yuxiu and Li Xinyang, sued Ju Runsheng and others in the Civil Division of the French Court for ignoring advances related to the Yi Sheng Zhuang. Yesterday, a witness was called to testify. Yu Qiaqing stated that during the takeover and sale of Yi Sheng Zhuang twenty-four years ago, merchants at the scene testified that Yi Sheng Zhuang had over one million in outstanding orders, which was precarious. Fearing that Rui Kang Hao would be affected, Zhao Yuting, the plaintiff's uncle, who was over sixty years old, took over the takeover and sale of Yi Sheng Zhuang to be run by the plaintiff to ensure the greater good. However, the internal situation was not entirely clear to the merchants. The plaintiff's lawyer asked if Zhao Runji was the same as Ju Runsheng. Yu replied that Zhao Runji was Zhao Shuangting. The plaintiff, Zhao Guanqing, claimed that the defendant, Ju Runsheng, was actually a shareholder of Yi Sheng Zhuang, attached to his uncle, Zhao Yuting, and thus Zhao Runji came forward to take over the operation and sales of the business to him. At the time, the merchants taking over the business were fully aware they would lose, and were even aware they could face imprisonment. Out of deference to his uncle, coupled with Yu Qiaqing's gentle persuasion, he was willing to endure the loss and agreed to find a way to compensate for it later. Unexpectedly, after the death of his uncle Zhao Shuangting, the defendant Ju Runsheng only provided compensation of over fifty thousand yuan, refusing to provide further compensation which was deliberately intended to be deceitful and excessively deceptive. Yu Qiaqing further stated that at that time, the merchants were indeed aware that Guanqing was incurring significant losses and had indeed agreed to compensate him later. Afterwards, Zhao Yuting transferred fifty thousand yuan to compensate Zhao Guanqing which was a fact. Ju Runsheng, represented by lawyer Lu Shaozong, argued that Yu Qiaqing had testified that Zhao Runji was Zhao Yuting, thus indicating that his client, Ju Runsheng, had no relationship with Yi Sheng Zhuang. He continued to argue that the plaintiff and defendant were relatives, the plaintiff Zhao Guanqing being the nephew of the defendant Ju Runsheng. Because Zhao Guanqing often asked Ju Runsheng for large sums of money, the plaintiff Zhao Guanqing had previously attempted to borrow one hundred thousand yuan from Ju Runsheng, and after being denied what he desired, insulted him. Afterwards, upon mediation, he eventually borrowed fifty thousand yuan, with the plaintiff sending a letter of apology. He now presents the letter for inspection. He claims that this suit is an attempt to blackmail and there are no other disputes, requesting that the case be dismissed. The plaintiff's lawyer then argued that the value of the case was a total of 459,000 taels, and the amount of damages

was estimated at over a million yuan. The defendant has limited real estate. The judge Gong ruled that the witness had already been heard and the case was adjourned to a later date for further arguments.

Bicycle Theft Incident 196

Stopped by the Shop Owner Outside

Sentenced to Four Months Imprisonment

Li Ronggen, from Yixing, rented a bicycle from Liu Xingyu's bicycle shop at 2600 Yangshupu Road on the morning of the first of this month at 10:00 AM. He rode it to the front of the cigarette and paper shop at 816 Taopeng Road. Li got off the bicycle and entered the shop, claiming he wanted to exchange silver dollars. The shop owner, Wang Laifu, was out, so Wang's wife came forward to transact the business. Li, seeing that the woman was easily deceived, jumped into the shop and robbed thirty-six cents in coins from the counter. He did not have time to take any more. He then jumped on the original bicycle and fled. At that time, Wang Laifu, the shop owner, was returning from outside and saw Li fleeing from the shop. Hearing his wife shouting "thief," he immediately stopped Li and handed him over to the Chinese constable at 1944. The constable searched him and found the stolen goods. Yesterday morning, the plaintiff and Liu Xingyu were summoned and brought before the Special District Court. After questioning by Judge Xiao, Li was sentenced to four months of imprisonment. The bicycle was returned to Liu Xingyu.

Maltreatment of a Child Bride Causes Public Outrage 197

Little Yangzi Suffers All Kinds of Hardship

Wang Gu's Family Arrested by Officials

Wang Lumeng, from Xinghua, lives on a boat at the Huiguan Wharf in the South City. He has a son who is currently fourteen years old. Seven years ago, a female fellow villager named Gu brought her daughter, Little Yangzi (now thirteen years old), to the Wang family to be a child bride due to hardship in their hometown. Wang's wife, Gu, is forty-nine years old and is inherently violent. Throughout the year, regardless of wind or snow, she forces Little Yangzi to go out and scavenge and even to steal. If Little Yangzi slightly displeases her, she is whipped,

leaving her covered in injuries and living in a hellish situation all day long. Yesterday afternoon at around 1:00 PM, Gu again beat her arbitrarily on the wharf because she did not bring back valuable items from scavenging in the morning, and prevented her from crying out. A large crowd gathered to watch, and seeing this situation, they felt aggrieved and stepped forward to dissuade her. However, Gu instead cursed at them, saying it was none of their business, which aroused public anger. The crowd immediately reported the incident to Xiao Enpei, the watchman at the 15th post in the area. Xiao Enpei detained Gu and took her along with Little Yangzi to the First Section of the First District, where the section chief questioned her during a preliminary hearing. Wang Gu confessed that she had given twelve yuan

Page 16

and one dou of white rice and six bolts of cloth to marry Little Yangzi as a daughter-in-law. Since she was the aunt, she was only giving slight discipline to Little Yangzi when she did not perform her duties properly. It was observed that Little Yangzi had injuries all over her body and a swollen face. The case involved injury, and an official report was prepared and submitted to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for further investigation.

Counterfeiting "White Lady" Brand Perfume 198

Four Months Imprisonment and a Thousand Yuan Fine

Li Zhaofen Unhappy and Has Appealed

"White Lady" brand hair tonic manufactured by the British Atkinson Limited has been exclusively distributed by Lulin & Co. on Jiangxi Road in this city for many years. Ladies from all walks of life enjoy purchasing this item as a cosmetic for its high quality and fragrant aroma. However, Li Zhaofen, a Cantonese shareholder and manager of Qichang Company, was seized by greed. He imitated and sold counterfeit products. The trademarks pasted on the bottles were especially similar. The drawing on the Lulin bottle is printed on green paper and shows a white-clothed maiden standing gracefully, with a long skirt trailing on the ground, her feet hidden and her head resembling a flying canopy, holding a violin and pretending to play it. The upper, lower, and middle sections of the drawing are printed in Western languages. The drawing on the Qichang bottle is also printed on green paper and shows a white-clothed maiden standing next to it, but her clothes only reach her knees and she is wearing leather shoes. This is slightly different, but other features such as her short, frizzy hair and the musical instrument she is holding are almost identical. If buyers do not examine the products carefully, it will be difficult to distinguish between the genuine and counterfeit products. Lulin & Co. only recently discovered the counterfeit products on the market. If they are not strictly investigated, it will have a significant impact on their business. Furthermore, the hair tonic they distribute has already been registered and should be protected by the government. It is inappropriate for others to imitate it, so they specially reported the case to the police for a secret investigation. The Hui Division Police Department investigated and confirmed that the factory where Qichang Company was counterfeiting the cosmetic products was located at 239 to 241 Haining Road, and the distribution point was located in a certain room at 141 Tiantong Road. The police dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to search both locations last Thursday. They seized over eighty large boxes of counterfeit hair tonic, printed trademark drawings, and empty bottles for filling the water. In addition, they also seized genuine drawings from Lulin & Co., presumably used as models for the counterfeit products. Li Zhaofen was arrested and handed over to the Special District Court. Judge Luo Renji ordered him to be released on bail of four thousand yuan in cash pending trial. The day before yesterday, Judge Luo Renji held a court hearing. Police lawyer Qian Xunji stated that the evidence in this case was sufficient and requested that he be punished for counterfeiting trademarks under Article 268 of the Criminal Code. Lulin & Co. also retained lawyers Lu Congzu and Wheeler to appear in court and stated that they would like to reserve the private prosecution portion of the case. The defendant only admitted to imitating and claimed that it was not counterfeiting, and he retained a lawyer to defend him. Subsequently, the lawyers for both the plaintiff and the victim presented various legal arguments based on the interpretation of the Judicial Yuan, proving that imitation was no different from counterfeiting. Judge Luo then repeatedly reviewed the genuine and counterfeit trademark drawings submitted as evidence and determined that the defendant's counterfeiting was indeed true. He immediately sentenced him to four months of imprisonment and imposed a fine of one thousand yuan as a warning. The defendant declared in court that he would appeal. The plaintiff's lawyer stated that if the defendant requested bail during the appeal period, the bail amount should be increased. The defendant increased the cash bail by three thousand yuan, totaling seven thousand yuan, and was allowed to be released on bail pending appeal review.

Pre-Arbitration Consultation on the Sinking of the Dachang 200

Preliminary Issues for the Arbitrators

Following the sinking of the Dachang vessel after being struck by the Dahua vessel, the matter of liability is to be submitted to arbitration. The Dahua and Pingan companies have jointly requested the Shanghai Shipping Association to establish the arbitration regulations and the arbitration committee. Now, Pingan Company asserts that the managers of both parties should be the arbitration representatives, with the Association appointing another representative. Dahua Company, however, contends that the managers are not shipping experts and that specialists should be appointed instead. The correspondence between the two parties is as follows:

Pingan Company Letter: In response to your company's letter of May 29th, which stated that both parties should send a responsible representative to the Shipping Association to discuss the terms of the arbitration agreement, we are in agreement and have been instructed by your company to promptly set a date. We must clarify that the so-called responsible representative refers to the managers of both companies. In addition to the managers of both parties discussing the terms in person, we also request that the Shipping Association send a representative to attend. No other person may participate. If there is no objection, please have the Shipping Association select a date and notify both parties one week in advance. Addressed to: Dahua Company, from Pingan Company, June 5th.

Dahua Company Letter: In response to your company's letter of the 5th of this month regarding the section that both parties should send a responsible representative to the Shipping Association to discuss the terms of the arbitration agreement. It mentioned that the so-called responsible representative refers to the managers of both companies. In addition to the managers of both parties discussing the terms in person, we also request that the Shipping Association send a representative to attend, and no other person may participate. We must say, that the responsible representative, while the managers of both parties have never not been an element that can be delegated, it must be viewed if a person is capable of fulfilling their role or not. If it must be the managers of both companies, it would be a limited view that they would be able to restrict one another and that this makes one suspicious of the narrow view, and how easily this is handled. Regarding this contract representative, it concerns the continuation of the arbitration to the point that it is of great importance, and the interest of the company in this situation has a intimate relationship. It is appropriate to choose who has the most outstanding and clear view of reason to take on this role. To handle the situation formally it would be free of any oversight that the internal transfer of workers of the company could deal with it to the sufficient extent. In this role, it does not necessarily need to be a company manager. If the company managers are competent, that will do, otherwise it would work to have other people be competent. The term responsible representative, entails to shoulder the responsibility for the whole situation. Should this person be someone whose qualifications are someone the company trusts they would already be appointed by the company freely. Therefore, the agreement of the other would not be necessary. So wherefore this limitation for the other party? In national regulations the court still works this way. We would think that your company would not be stubborn in their views and would generously include them. Thus, aside from saying that the representatives of both sides does not have to only be the company managers, to respect the issues surrounding this contract, and to better gather ideas and incorporate legal issues, there is a proposal: to designate two responsible representatives and one legal advisor/lawyer of legal representatives to be sent by each company. Again, this is to be assigned by the shipping association for one last representative to attend. If agreed, both sides can send a letter to the union to select a date a week in advance to notify the people to attend this conference, to facilitate both parties to arrange the handlings for the procedure, which is more thorough and the dispositions are fair. There will not be any more unexpected twists and turns. If your company is not of this opinion and awaits other conditions, then we may consider submitting this proposal to the Union in advance to resolve to avoid the delay that would hinder this affair of public interest. Addressed to Ping An Company, from Dahua Company

The Planning and Construction of Huibing Bridge on the Songhu Road 201

Since construction began, the northern part of Shanghai on Songhu Road has been largely completed and is now being paved with gravel, so the completion of the entire road is imminent. The Shanghai County Construction Bureau has now found that there is a Huibing Bridge located at the intersection of Songjiang and Shanghai on the road. It was destroyed in the Jiazi Rebellion, cutting off land traffic. Now that the northern part of the road in this county is about to be completed and Songjiang is also under construction, the construction of the Huibing Bridge is imperative. Furthermore, long-distance buses on the Songhu Road are preparing to operate. Director Wu, in accordance with the promulgated drawings, designed a concrete and steel bridge. However, the estimated cost is very large, and the construction funds in this county have been almost completely depleted, making fundraising difficult. Yesterday, Wu submitted a document to the county government along with the bridge drawings and budget, requesting that it be forwarded to the Jiangsu Construction Department for review and approval.

Meeting Minutes of the Accountants Association 202

The Shanghai Accountants Association held its 19th Executive Committee meeting yesterday. Commissioner Jiang Wanping chaired the meeting. The Standing Committee proposed that since the association's emblem has been exhausted and the government has issued new regulations requiring professional associations to use rectangular emblems, the association's emblem should not continue to be produced in the old style. It was decided that for the sake of receiving and accounting for money there needs to be an official receipt for what's being issued. At 6 o'clock the meeting adjourned.

Yangjing Town Chiefs and Police Pay Attention to Gambling and Opium 206

The chiefs and police officers of the second section of the third district of Yangjing Town have recently become more diligent in their duties. They patrol the old and new opium dens and gambling houses, disguised or waiting in ambush day and night. A few days ago, when searching Pan Axiang's and A Tong's opium dens, the dispatched chiefs and police officers fearlessly climbed onto the roof and broke down walls, as if facing a major enemy. None escaped. As a result, four opium dens and two gambling houses have been raided in recent days, and thirty to forty opium users and gamblers have been arrested. The town's atmosphere of drugs and gambling has been slightly curbed. However, cases of theft in the countryside are still frequent. If the chiefs and police officers paid more attention, the residents would be even more grateful.

Weather Report 209

The Zikawei Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the weather in the Yangtze River basin and the coast here is changing and there is light fog due to a low-pressure center formed between the Yellow River and the Yangtze River. There are south to southwest winds of varying degrees on the Shandong coast, and south to southeast winds of varying degrees in the Yangtze River. The southeast is light and unstable. Also, in the 24 hours before 3 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in the local area was 81.3 and the lowest was 61.2. On the same day last year, the highest was 83.3 and the lowest was 63.0.

Theater News 211

Lianhua Film Company declares that since the establishment of the company's music and dance troupe in February of this year, it has actively improved and achieved remarkable results. Last month, it was invited to perform at the Capital Grand Theater in Nanjing and was highly praised by the people of the capital. It returned to Shanghai with honor. The Odeon Theater in this city heard of its reputation and specially hired it to perform publicly at the theater starting today (the 9th). The head of the troupe, Mr. Li Jinhui, is the founder of Chinese song and dance drama. Every time he creates a play, the whole country follows suit because its taste is profound, pure, and difficult for the vulgar to appreciate. The ten or so musicians have more than ten years of training, and their skills have reached perfection. The instruments used are both Chinese and Western, and are all famous in the north and south. The members of the Bright Moon Opera Society and the direct disciples of Li's father and daughter have voices as melodious as orioles outside the willows and dances as graceful as butterflies among the flowers. The power it reveals can penetrate the hearts of the audience and stir their emotions. Moreover, this public performance at the Cantonese Odeon Lin Theater will feature more than sixty new costumes and newly compiled programs. Its sensation in Shanghai is a matter of course. Those who love to watch can book seats at the theater in advance to avoid regrets at the last minute.

Social News

The Ninetieth Birthday of the London Library 212

— Translated by Fu Lan

The world-famous London Library celebrated its ninetieth anniversary at the beginning of last month. In 1841, it occupied only two rooms and had only three thousand books. Ninety years later, the library stands majestically on St. James's Square, with over 450,000 books. Looking back on the past, it is truly worth commemorating.

Dr. C. T. Hagbery Wright has been the librarian of the library since 1893 and is the most experienced and qualified librarian. He recently gave an interview to the London Morning Post, stating the London Library's two golden rules: (1) never buy a new novel, and (2) never sell a book.

(We do not want to satisfy readers' fleeting needs for new novels, he said. (We do not want to compete with commercial lending libraries, so we have made a rule that we will not buy a novel until it has been published for less than six months, and we will never buy more than three copies of the same book in the future.

(If readers come to ask to read a book on the day it is published and we want to satisfy everyone's needs, then the library may not be able to stand firm. For example, several years ago, almost two thousand members simultaneously requested a biography of Lord Roberts. We would have had to purchase two thousand copies, which would have resulted in a huge loss.

(No matter how great the novelist's reputation is, we must wait six months after publication before we buy his books. Even Thackeray and T. Hardy cannot escape this exception.

(I have also made a rule), he said, (never sell or destroy a book. In certain circumstances, when the need for a certain book seems to have disappeared, we put these books in the (cold palace) and let them stay there for seven years. If there is still no need for them during this period, then we send them to the library in Sicily.)

In the past ninety years, the characteristics of the London Library have remained the same, but the people who read have changed. In 1841, women accounted for only three percent of the members, but now they account for a larger proportion.

In the first year of the London Library's establishment, Carlyle and Macanley were both fully engrossed in the library. Carlyle had a bad habit of borrowing books and often refusing to return them. In addition, Gladstone prepared the first step of his religious history in the library. Thackeray's inspection of the books for two years was a valuable record.

The most dangerous period in the history of the London Library was the Crimean War. At that time, the number of members decreased to an alarming number in a short period of time, so the purchase of new books was temporarily suspended.

It currently has more than four thousand members and no longer worries about standing firm. It is now planning the construction of new buildings to store the steady stream of new books from 1931 to 2081.

The Eastern News Records the Chinese Silk Industry 213

Mr. Shiohara lists the advantages and disadvantages of silkworm rearing and silk reeling. According to the Eastern News, Mr. Katsumi Shiohara, the director of the Suwa Silk Reeling Research Association in Japan, recently inspected the Chinese silk industry and visited the silk industry in Beijing, Hangzhou, and Suzhou before returning. He said that China has a vast land and mulberry trees grow very well, so there is great hope for it to become a silk country in the future. However, there are also many shortcomings due to the Chinese national character and national conditions. Japan is afraid of what it needs to be afraid of in the distant future. The shortcomings of China's silkworm rearing aspect are: (1) the structure of the silkworm rearing house is not suitable for breeding, and its transformation is difficult due to various circumstances; (2) no artificial prevention methods are used for the climate; (3) silkworm varieties are weak in resistance to low temperature and high humidity. Its advantages are: (1) mulberry trees grow very well; (2) silkworm varieties are still suitable for seriprene-based silk quality; (3) labor costs are low, about 1.1 to 1.5 yuan per day. The shortcomings of silk reeling are: (1) silk reeling methods are poor, and cocoon cooking is especially poor; (2) the construction and improvement of factories are about four times more expensive than the price of village wood. Its characteristics are: (1) compared to the poor cocoons, the raw silk fineness is fine and the annual knots are still good; (2) all expenses are borne by women, about 0.3 yuan or less to about 0.1 yuan; (3) the silk reeling machine, six or seven seats, is a French iron product, far superior to Japan. In addition, the facilities of public silk improvement farms are quite amazing, but the silkworm rearers and silk reelers in the private sector are deeply superstitious and quite naive.

Algerian Matches Beaten Down by Russian Goods 214

Two factories closed, one reduced exports by 70 percent

Paris News: The dumping of Soviet industrial products abroad is all-encompassing. The European market has been greatly affected. The match industry in French Algeria has gradually become unable to stand firm in recent years due to the squeeze of Russian goods. The Algerian Chamber of Commerce recently requested the French government to take measures to protect it. Major newspapers in Paris, such as the Morning News, etc., strongly advocated taking strong actions to restrict the import of Soviet matches into Algeria and restrict the import of general Russian goods into France. Algeria has a large match factory, one of which has been closed and the other has also reduced shipments, barely maintaining it. In the past three years, the amount of Algerian matches exported to other French colonies has fallen by 70 percent, all due to the invasion of Russian goods. According to the Morning News, Russian matches are masquerading as Algerian matches in boxes with the Algerian label. Algerian consumers cannot distinguish them. Even the Algerian match manufacturers initially did not suspect their origin. It was only after a long time that they discovered that they were Russian goods. French newspapers also reported that the United States and Belgium impose heavy taxes on foreign matches, and the United Kingdom is also considering methods.

Marshal Foch's War Diary 215

— Translated by Gu Angruo

The German attack on March 21st wanted to cut off the British and French lines. The first step of our army was to quickly stop it. After success, the second step was to systematically arrange defense lines and compile reserve troops to consolidate the new positions. The important task after this was to recover the lost land to ensure that the supply of military and civilian food was not harmed by the enemy.

Therefore, on April 3rd, I ordered Commander-in-Chief Haig and General Pétain to set up a strong defense line north of the Somme River and take an offensive south of the Somme River to relieve the crisis in Amiens. In principle, April 12th was decided as the date of attack, but we expected that it would not be possible to implement it as scheduled.

On April 9th, another major battle broke out in Armentières. On that day, the German Fourth Army (led by Sixt von Armin) attacked the positions between Bixschoote and Armentières with nine divisions. The defending soldiers were three British divisions and one Portuguese division belonging to the British First Army (led by Horne).

While the troops were being transferred, they were suddenly attacked by the enemy. The Portuguese division was caught off guard and was defeated. The British defense line was cut off and the enemy directly forced their way to Laventie from the center. They were eventually attacked and progressed to the Lys River between Estaires and Sailly-sur-la-Lys. On the 10th, the enemy continued to attack and joined five new divisions. They developed north to Messines. Therefore, the enemy's attack range included the right wing of the British Second Army (led by Plumer), Armentières and Messines fell one after another. The enemy then crossed the Lys River. The battle line stretched for fifteen miles from Doulieu to Estaires, advancing westward towards Hazebrouck.
